\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01213}01213\ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }test\_chi\_square\_kernel():}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01214}01214\ \ \ \ \ rng\ =\ np.random.RandomState(0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01215}01215\ \ \ \ \ X\ =\ rng.random\_sample((5,\ 4))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01216}01216\ \ \ \ \ Y\ =\ rng.random\_sample((10,\ 4))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01217}01217\ \ \ \ \ K\_add\ =\ additive\_chi2\_kernel(X,\ Y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01218}01218\ \ \ \ \ gamma\ =\ 0.1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01219}01219\ \ \ \ \ K\ =\ chi2\_kernel(X,\ Y,\ gamma=gamma)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01220}01220\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{assert}\ K.dtype\ ==\ float}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01221}01221\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ i,\ x\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ enumerate(X):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01222}01222\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ j,\ y\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ enumerate(Y):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01223}01223\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ chi2\ =\ -\/np.sum((x\ -\/\ y)\ **\ 2\ /\ (x\ +\ y))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2metrics_2tests_2test__pairwise_8py_source_l01224}01224\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ chi2\_exp\ =\ np.exp(gamma\ *\ chi2)}
